 ab cook ne tay kiya ki is duusare sebar vimaan kaa peechha karnaa bekaar he, jo aakhirkaar aisi haalat main apane base kii taraf bhaag gaya, jiske baad vah dobaaraa shaayad kabhi nahin ud paaya hoga

 " Significantly, air battles have been quite rare since the Second World War, and very few pilots have a chance to join one dogfight in their careers, while our Alfred Cook was going to join his third dogfight in a single day , And the interesting fact is that this Tusri dogfight was also not the last
 pashchim bengal ke akaash main ab teesraa sebar vimaan cook ke peeche tha, so, unhone sahi posishan main aane ke liye ghota lagaaya
 He had to make sharp turns for him, and use the power of his Hawker Hunter aircraft engine to follow the enemy

 The His plane went away, and i worried about why he didn't fire
 
 
 tabhi mujhe ehsaas hua ki zamin kaaphi nazadik aa chuki he

 aap chunki 100 goliyaan prati second kii raftaar se firing kar rahe hote hai, so, us gote se baahar aate-aate hi meraa aslaa khatm ho gaya, or main zamin se takaraate-takaraate bachaa
 
 
 " teesraa pakistani sebar vimaan bhaagane main kaamyaab ho gaya, or cook ko bhi is baat se puri tasalli thi, kyonki unke paas aslaa khatm ho chukaa tha, lekin hawaii ladaai main apane vingamain kaa dhyaan rakhana hi khaas gur he

 or phir maine use (dushman ko) ulajhaa liya or ham yah sab airfield par bane flying control ke thik upar kar rahe the

 "tippaniyan But Cook could not attack the Pakistani aircraft, because there was not a single bullet left
 iske bajaae vah uske thik peeche lage rahe, or lagaataar nishane par rakhkar use bhartiya seemaa ke baahar khaded diya
 Cook, who came to Hindustan to attend the event that marked the completion of 50 years of the 1965 war, looked smiling lost in the memories of his last battle, and said of the Pakistani pilot, "he must have known that his fate that day was very good Was
 
 
 " Both Cook and Mamgai were awarded the Vir Chakra

 lekin dushmano ke saath sirf 12 hi minute kii ladaai main yah saaf ho gaya tha ki sitambar, 1965 main hamaari vayusena ko ek nayaa hero mil gaya

 so, turant upar gaya, tikhaa daayan mode liya, rukaa or duusare vimaan se bhid gaya
 
 
 " duusare vimaan se hui dogphite ko cook 'intence' (joardaar) bataate hai
 In fact, during the war that took place with this aircraft, Cook was getting so close to the Pakistani aircraft that the danger of collision of both planes in the air was coming again and again

 " "main uskaa cheharaa dekh saktaa tha, or vah meraa

 i suddenly went down a lot, and taking advantage of reaching a good position, started firing bullets as soon as he came under target
 
 
 main jaanata tha, use goliyaan lag rahi hai, or mujhe ummid thi ki uskaa vimaan ab fat jayega
 
 
 " lekin aisa nahin hua
 Cook's entire high-exploratory asylum was over, and now he had only ball-ammunition left, which is commonly used for training
 so, cook ke waar karne or pakistani jet ko hamale se nuksaan hone ke baavjood vah abhi tak ud rahaa tha
 Now Cook decided that it was useless to chase down this second Saber aircraft, which eventually ran towards his base in such a condition, after which he might have never flown again
 "vah lagaataar mujhase dur bhaagane kii koshish kar rahaa tha, or achaanak maine dekha, vah pehle kii tulana main zyaada neeche dive karne laga he, so, sabase pehle mere dimag main aayaa ki shaayad kisi ne use chetaya he, or mere peeche koi or he
 
 
 " gauratlab he ki duusare vishwayuddh ke baad se hawaii ladaaiyaan kaaphi durlabh hai, or bahut kam payalton ke hi kariyar main kisi ek dogphite main shaamil hone kaa mauka aata he, jabaki hamaare alfred cook ek hi din main apni teesri dogphite main shaamil hone ja rahe the, or dilachasp tathy yah he ki yah tuusari dogphite bhi aakhri nahin thi
 The third Saber plane was now behind Cook in the West Bengal sky, so he dived to get in the right position
 unhen uske liye tikhaa mode lene the, or apane hoker hunter vimaan ke ingine kii takat kaa istemaal karnaa tha, taaki dushman ke peeche aa saken
 According to Cook, "I was coming from top to bottom with the bullets on him, and was wondering, why the target is not targeted, why his plane is not exploding
" 
 
 ? uskaa vimaan dur ho gaya, or mujhe is baat kii chintaa thi ki use goliyaan lagi kyon nahin
 
 
 Then i realized that the land has come very close
 
 
 meri anguliyaan tab bhi trigar par thim, so, maine turant joistic ko waapas khinchaa, lekin durbhaagya se tab tak mere paas maujuud sara aslaa khatm ho gaya tha, kyonki hunter vimaanon par hamaara firing time lagbhag paanch second kaa hi hota he
 
 
 Since you are firing at 100 bullets per second, my slack came to an end when i came out of that ditch, and i survived hitting the ground
 
 
 " The third Pakistani Saber plane managed to escape, and Cook was also comforted by this, because he had finished the asylum, but in air combat, it is a special skill to take care of his wigman
 flying officer essi mamgai kii jaan puri tarah khatre main thi, kyonki ek sebar vimaan thik unke peeche pahunch chukaa tha, lekin cook halaat kii taraf puri tarah chaukanne the
 He told, "I warned Mamgai
 
 
 maine kaha 'mam break port' (bain taraf tikhaa mode kaato)
 
 
 And then i entangled him (the enemy) and we were doing all this right above the flying control on the airfield
 
 
 usne mujhase peechha chhudaane ke liye loop or kalabaziyaan shuru kar deen, lekin us vakt meraa vimaan halkaa tha, or chunki aisi kalabaziyaan ham masti ke liye karte hi rahete the, so, mujhe uske peeche lage rahane main koi dikkat nahin hui
 
 
 "comments lekin cook us pakistani vimaan par waar nahin kar paae, kyonki ek bhi goli bachi hi nahin thi
 Instead, he followed her right away, and kept her out of the Indian border, constantly on target
 1965 yuddh ke 50 saal puure hone par yojit kaarykram main hissaa lene hindustan aae cook apni aakhri ladaai kii yaadon main khoe hue muskuraate dikhe, or us pakistani payalat ke bare main bole, "use pakkaa pataa chal gaya hoga ki us din uskaa bhagya bahut acha tha
 
 
 " cook or mamgai, donon ko vir chakra pradaan kiya gaya
 Cook flew fighter jets a few years after that, and then moved to Australia
 haalanki unhone baad main chote naagarik vimaan udaae, lekin 740 kilometre prati ghante kii raftaar se zamin se sirf 10 foot upar hoker hunter vimaan udaane jaisaa tajurba phir nahin mil saktaa
 
 
 a dogfight from another plane is described by Cook as 'intense'
 darasal, is vimaan se jo yuddh hua, uske dauraan cook pakistani vimaan ke itnaa kareeb ja rahe the ki hawa main donon vimaanon kii takkar hone kaa khatra baar-baar sane aa rahaa tha
 Cook, who settled in Australia four years after the 1965 war, recalled during his recent visit to Delhi, "we were so close to each other that we could see each other's face
" 
 
 " "I could see his face, and that mine
 
 
 mujhe uskaa helmet dikh rahaa tha, safed helmet, jis par uskaa naam likhaa tha
 
 
 i also had a white helmet on my head with my name written on it
 
 
 main achaanak bahut neeche gaya, or acchhee posishan main pahunch jane kaa phayda uthaate hue uske nishane par aate hi goliyaan chalaani shuru kar deen
 
 
 i knew, he was fired, and i expected his plane to explode now
 
 
 " but that did not happen
 cook kaa sara hai-explosive aslaa khatm ho gaya, or ab unke paas sirf ball-amunishan bachaa tha, jo aamtaur par training ke liye istemaal kiya jaataa he
 So, despite Cook's blows and Pakistani jet losses from the attack, he was still flying
 ab cook ne tay kiya ki is duusare sebar vimaan kaa peechha karnaa bekaar he, jo aakhirkaar aisi haalat main apane base kii taraf bhaag gaya, jiske baad vah dobaaraa shaayad kabhi nahin ud paaya hoga
 "he was constantly trying to run away from me, and suddenly i saw, he started diving down more than before, so first thing came to my mind that maybe someone has warned him, and someone else behind me is
 
 
 " Significantly, air battles have been quite rare since the Second World War, and very few pilots have a chance to join one dogfight in their careers, while our Alfred Cook was going to join his third dogfight in a single day , And the interesting fact is that this Tusri dogfight was also not the last
 pashchim bengal ke akaash main ab teesraa sebar vimaan cook ke peeche tha, so, unhone sahi posishan main aane ke liye ghota lagaaya
 He had to make sharp turns for him, and use the power of his Hawker Hunter aircraft engine to follow the enemy
 cook ke anusaar, "main us par goliyaan barsaata hua upar se neeche kii ore aa rahaa tha, or soch rahaa tha, nishaanaa lag kyon nahin rahaa he, uske vimaan main visphot kyon nahin ho rahaa he
 
 
 The His plane went away, and i worried about why he didn't fire
 
 
 tabhi mujhe ehsaas hua ki zamin kaaphi nazadik aa chuki he
 
 
 My fingers were still on the trigger, so i immediately pulled the joystick back, but unfortunately by then all the slug i had was gone, because our firing time on Hunter planes is only about five seconds
 
 
 aap chunki 100 goliyaan prati second kii raftaar se firing kar rahe hote hai, so, us gote se baahar aate-aate hi meraa aslaa khatm ho gaya, or main zamin se takaraate-takaraate bachaa
 
 
 " teesraa pakistani sebar vimaan bhaagane main kaamyaab ho gaya, or cook ko bhi is baat se puri tasalli thi, kyonki unke paas aslaa khatm ho chukaa tha, lekin hawaii ladaai main apane vingamain kaa dhyaan rakhana hi khaas gur he
 Flying Officer SC Mamgai's life was in complete danger, as a Saber aircraft had reached right behind him, but Cook was fully alert to the situation
 unhone bataaya, "maine mamgai ko chetavanee di
 
 
 i said 'mam break port'
 
 
 or phir maine use (dushman ko) ulajhaa liya or ham yah sab airfield par bane flying control ke thik upar kar rahe the
 
 
 He started doing loops and acrobats to get rid of me, but my plane was light at the time, and since we used to do such acrobats for fun, i had no problem following him
 
 
 "tippaniyan But Cook could not attack the Pakistani aircraft, because there was not a single bullet left
 iske bajaae vah uske thik peeche lage rahe, or lagaataar nishane par rakhkar use bhartiya seemaa ke baahar khaded diya
 Cook, who came to Hindustan to attend the event that marked the completion of 50 years of the 1965 war, looked smiling lost in the memories of his last battle, and said of the Pakistani pilot, "he must have known that his fate that day was very good Was

 The most common type is diabetes
 uske baad he jestational diabetes (garbhavastha ke dauraan hone vaali diabetes)

 ilaaj na karne par iske kaaran ankhon, gurde or nason par asar padane lagata he

 pairon kii ore rakt kaa pravaah kam ho jaataa he or pair kaatane tak kii sthiti bhi aa jaati he

 For the treatment of diabetes, it is necessary to change lifestyle, dietary restraint, exercising, taking pills / injections or insulin
 diabetes ke rogiyon ko atyadhik calories vaali yaa sharkara badhaane vaali chijen jaise mithai, soft drink se parhez karnaa chahie

 diabetes ke rogi insulin ke naam se hi darate hai

e
 decrease in blood sugar is common and can be life threatening

 drink karne ke baad sharir main bahut zyada dihydration ho jaataa he
 So drink as much water as possible to keep hydrated
 hangover kam karne ke lienariyal pani or subjiyon se bana soupabhi pilaa sakate hai
 2
 drink karne se sharir main blad sugar kaa level kam ho jaataa he
 Sweet things should be served the next day after drinking
 3
 Lemon, orange and guava should be eaten in order to remove the hangover
 neembu pani pinaa bhi phydemand hota he
 4
 kele ko shahad or doodh ke saath milakar khaane se sharir kii pachan kriya darust rahati he
 Along with this, it reduces the hangover and gives strength to the body

 jisase sarkaar or aalaa afasar pareshaan ho gaye the

 rajya kii kul 224 vidhansabha siton main se 57 siten dakshini karnataka kshetra se aati hai

 devgauda vokkaliga samudaay se aate hai, jabaki siddharmaiya korba samudaay se
